<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Payten provides complete payment industry solutions, for non-financial and financial institutions, supporting card and card-less transactions. We run our business in South Eastern Europe, Spain, Portugal, Andorra, Columbia, Peru, Dominican Republic and Egypt and are actively selling on other markets.
The offering includes solutions for eCommerce, mPayments, Processing as well as ATM and POS related services. We deliver software and services including outsourcing and equipment, providing highest level of expertise, maintenance and support through the entire portfolio.

Payten in numbers:

• Close to 150 clients relying on ASEE POS/ATM services and apps
• 65+MM eCommerce transactions processed per month and active outside SEE region
• 5,5+MM tokenization transactions processed per month 
• 15+MM card transactions processed per month
• 9,500 + ATMs successfully maintained
• 600,000 POS units in 16 countries

Although Payten brand is new in the Asseco group it has a track record of strong performance and satisfied clients of the Asseco South Eastern Europe Payment Business Unit it has derived from. It is a member of the Asseco South Eastern Europe group (ASEE), a leading IT provider in the SEE region in terms of the revenue derived from its own software and services. Covering 22 countries, ASEE is the top player for banking and strong in other industrial verticals. It employs more than 2755 employees and is part of the Asseco Group, which ranks among top ten software vendors in Europe.

          </p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">💥 Payten in Chișinău for the first time — GOLD Sponsor at Fintech Moldova Conference 2025. Speaker Ciprian Pirv.

On October 3, meet us at Digital Park, Chișinău, alongside ~400 leaders from banking, fintech, and the public sector. The agenda spotlights the Future of Payments, developments in Open Banking/Instant Payments, and cyber-resilience in financial services.

Why this matters: as a GOLD Sponsor, Payten brings expanded exposure, stage time, and panel participation—the right setting for practical conversations with partners and clients.

🎙️ Join <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/ciprian-pirv?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ciprian Pirv</a> for a practical playbook on turning payments into outcomes: Payten’s end-to-end stack—eCommerce, mobile, processing, and ATM/POS—built to lift conversion, reduce acceptance costs, and harden resilience.

👉 Let’s meet in Chișinău, October 3—for actionable ideas, partnerships, and 1:1 discussions at the Payten booth (GOLD partners area).

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 Strengthening the Fintech Ecosystem in Romania and Beyond 🇷🇴🌍

At Payten, we believe that thriving ecosystems fuel innovation, growth, and opportunity. That’s why we are proud to support the Romanian Fintech Association – RoFintech, the key voice driving the development of the fintech industry in Romania and the region, by becoming their newest member. We’re not just joining an association — we’re bringing the power of Payten into the heart of Romania’s fintech transformation.

We see this partnership as an opportunity to accelerate progress, not just support it.

💥 What Payten brings to the table:
✅ Scalable, multi-bank payment platforms already powering top-tier retailers and financial institutions
✅ Real-world expertise in orchestrating complex, omnichannel payment environments
✅ A regional network that connects fintechs across borders and industries

For us it's a commitment to: 

🏗️ Strengthening the infrastructure that empowers fintechs to grow 

🔗 Connecting innovators, regulators, and established players 

🚀 Accelerating the digital transformation of financial services 

🌐 Building bridges between Romania’s fintech community and international markets

Every market where we operate has one thing in common — talented people with bold ideas. As a leading provider of payment technology across Europe, we see it as our responsibility to back those who are shaping the future of financial services. 

💡 Whether through technology, knowledge, or partnerships, we remain committed to empowering the fintech ecosystem — because when the ecosystem grows, we all move forward. 

📣 🇷🇴 From Romania to the rest of the region, Payten is here to shape what’s next in digital payments!

Let’s turn innovation into impact! Let’s build the future of fintech together — with purpose, speed, and ambition!

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 Thrilled to see the future of banking and payments being shaped at the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Funchain2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#UNCHAIN2025</a> roundtable — and proud that Payten was at the table through the voice of our own <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/ciprian-pirv?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ciprian Pirv</a>.

In a room full of bold thinkers and tech pioneers, Ciprian brought a grounded yet forward-looking perspective on:
🔹 How payment orchestration platforms are driving real impact for retailers and financial institutions
🔹 Why flexibility, speed, and provider-agnostic infrastructure are key to future-ready ecosystems
🔹 And what embedded and cross-border payments truly mean when translated into operational excellence

💬 At <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fpayten&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Payten</a>, we don’t just follow industry trends — we help shape them. This roundtable was proof that collaboration between banks, fintechs, and tech providers is critical to building what’s next.

Looking forward to the whitepaper and more shared innovation across the region.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">🏦 Banking and payments are evolving — from core services to building fully embedded financial ecosystems.

At <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Funchain2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#UNCHAIN2025</a>, selected guests gathered for a forward-looking roundtable on how banks and fintechs are reimagining the industry — exploring the future of core banking, real-world GenAI applications, SME-focused strategies, customer engagement beyond digital, the evolution of open banking, and building infrastructure for embedded and cross-border payments.

Moderated by <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/in/eliadsaporta?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Eliad Saporta</a>, the session brought together: <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/raul-chirulescu-1630648?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Raul Chirulescu</a> – Raiffeisen Bank; <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/ciprian-pirv?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ciprian Pirv</a> – Payten; <a class="link" href="https://cz.linkedin.com/in/martin-korbelar?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Martin Korbelar</a> – Tapix by Dateio; <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/gabrielpralea?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Gabriel Pralea</a> – CEC Bank; <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/nadezdabernikova?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nadia Bull Bernikova</a> – Silverflow; <a class="link" href="https://cz.linkedin.com/in/mvodrazka?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Michal Vodrážka</a> – Czech National Bank; <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/jessicauche?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Jessica Uche</a> – Native Teams; <a class="link" href="https://hu.linkedin.com/in/gaborgazso?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Gabor Gazso</a> – CARDSPOT.

The roundtable laid the groundwork for the innovations of the future — with CEE banking and payments leaders shaping what’s next for financial services.

📄 A white paper summarizing the key insights and future industry opportunities will follow.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">💡 Payment orchestration is no longer a “nice-to-have” — it’s the infrastructure behind a frictionless, competitive retail experience.
During today’s panel at UNCHAIN Festival — “Payments as a Competitive Advantage for Large Retailers” — we explored what orchestration really looks like in practice — beyond buzzwords.
🗣️ <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/pintilie-ionel-gabriel-900075b2?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Pintilie Ionel-Gabriel</a>, Payten Romania:
"Merchants today want flexibility, speed, and the ability to switch or combine providers — but without handling the complexity themselves. Our role is to take that complexity away, and give back control and visibility. That’s what orchestration should do.”
🛒 <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/dorin-branza-danciu-3532041?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Dorin Branza Danciu</a>, Auchan Romania:
"When you run hundreds of checkout lanes, adding a new payment method like BNPL or wallet solutions isn't just a tech upgrade — it's a business and operational challenge. Orchestration platforms help us integrate fast and keep a consistent customer experience across stores and channels.”
🎯 Key takeaways from the session:
✅ Orchestration is about control without chaos
✅ Large retailers need partners that speak both business and tech
✅ Success means building a scalable, flexible foundation – not chasing every trend
🙏 Huge thanks to <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/in/eliadsaporta?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Eliad Saporta</a> Sapora from <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fcoriunder&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Coriunder</a> for brilliantly moderating and weaving these perspectives into actionable takeaways for the audience!

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">💡 “Merchants want control. But control comes with complexity. And our job is to help them navigate that – without overwhelming them.” – <a class="link" href="https://ro.linkedin.com/in/ciprian-pirv?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ciprian Pirv</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fpayten&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Payten</a> Romania

Today at UNCHAIN Festival, during a forward-looking panel moderated by <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FbrdgroupesociAeztAezgAeznAezrale&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#BRDGroupeSociétéGénérale</a>, leaders from <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fpayten&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Payten</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fvisa&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#VISA</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsymphopay&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Symphopay</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftransfond&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Transfond</a> and BRD tackled a crucial question:
👉 How do we enable innovation in payments and liquidity management — without losing sight of what merchants truly need?
Ciprian brought a refreshing perspective:
🔄 We often talk about technology, features, and trends — but real value starts with giving merchants visibility and control over their processes.
⚙️ Yes, control brings complexity — but Payten’s mission is to absorb that complexity so merchants can build on a solid, flexible foundation.
🧩 Only then can they truly benefit from orchestration, instant payments, and next-gen treasury tools.

In a rapidly evolving financial landscape, this kind of merchant-first thinking is what makes innovation stick.
👏 Thank you BRD for the invitation and for hosting a panel that went beyond buzzwords and into real business transformation.

      <section class="aside-section-container mb-4" data-test-id="browse-jobs">

            <h2 class="aside-section-container__title section-title">
